<text>The staff here is friendly but Public Storages policies are not. They're designed to be unclear so that you owe more money. When I moved in I very clearly asked what the move out process was in regards to payment and was told that as long as I gave 2 days notice, I could move out whenever I liked (I now understand that this was a purposefully cryptic answer). I set my move out date online for September 1st over two weeks in advance, and at no point along the way during the move out process was it mentioned that I would owe the full amount for September by doing this. I was simply told to check in with the front desk when I completed my move out.

Of course, move out day comes and it turns out I owe the entirety of September, even though I am moving out on the 1st. The front desk staff were friendly enough about this but when I talked to the supervisor, Clare Ingram, and not only was she not able to help me, she was rude about it.

The company will try to claim they're not able to pro-rate payment, but they happily pro-rated my first month when I moved in. They also know damn well people move on the 1st. It's a policy that is designed to take advantage and the fact that there is no leeway despite a very understandable miscommunication is frustrating.

In addition to this, everything in the storage unit was covered in a thick layer of dust and sand after just 7 months. I know Lancaster is a windy dusty place, but when you're in the business of providing storage I think a little more could be done to insulate the spaces from this.

I won't be using Public Storage again in the future. I recommend you skip it as well.<//text><Name>Zen Zenith< /Name>< time>

My wife and I were victims of moving fraud; a broker from Miami teamed up with a very unscrupulous mover out of Los Angeles to basically steal from us.  After over a month of holding everything we own hostage, the mover just dumped all our household goods into two large storage units in Palmdale, CA.  Now our move was supposed to be from Draper, UT to Madison, MS, so how on earth everything we own ended up in California is still a puzzler.  Anyway, there were two bright spots (other than our lawyer) during this ordeal, and one was Frine, the manager of Public Storage in Palmdale.  She was awesome.  Between her and Claire, the district manager with Public Storage, we were able to successfully get control of our belongings again.  Frine and Claire were both understanding, sympathetic, and did everything they could give regulations, their policies and our circumstances, to make retrieval possible.  Thank you!<//Review>

<username>Sarah J</username>< review>
I have been a Public Storage customer in Palmdale, California, for over 7 years.  In March 2014, after renting a small space for over 5 years,I decided to move to a larger space.  Public Storage was having a special rate on one of their larger spaces for $91 per month.  I excitedly moved into this space, and less than 7 months later, I received a notice for an increase of $19, bringing the rental rate up to $110 per month.  I immediately called the corporate office, and the District Manager, Claire, to understand why there was an increase in less than a year, and to see if this this could be prevented.  Of course, no one could help me, and everyone I spoke with stated there was nothing that could be done, including the District Manager, Claire.

In September 2015, I received another notice for a rental increase of $10, effective October 1, 1015, bringing my total rental rate to $123.00.  I am outraged by this, and shocked that Public Storage continues to raise my rate without any regards for the fact that I have been a loyal customer, and also, because this is simply ridiculous.  I have hear over the years from several people who have rented spaces from Public Storage, and from employees who have stated this company does not care about it customers at all.  It is funny how no one at Public Storage could help me, but they have no problem raising their rates.

So, I am writing this review to warn everyone not to be lulled in by one of their "specials".  They took advantage of me, and I will be moving out of my space within the next 30 days.  I cannot continue to support a company who does not listen to the concerns or complaints of their customers, and one who raises rates needlessly, then tells customers there is nothing they can do.  Really?  This is a bunch of nonsense, and I repeat, DO NOT be taken in by their special deals because you will only have to pay more money in less than a year, and the rates will continue..

Good luck!</review>

< review>
The place needs a lil renovation.  Its really embarrassing to go in there where the couches are extremely soiled with broken springs and deflated seats. The carpets smell.
I do like their menu options compared to the rest of the campus.
But its pretty expensive for an on-campus bar.
When a glass of beer is $7 min, there's a problem.
I get it, you don't want drunk students bec you're offering $3 drinks,  but its also not your job to police students behaviors via prices.
Also 49ers as a company that services students with bookstores and on-campus venues,  seriously rips off the students.
Every single thing is marked up at least 50% more. Sometimes things cost twice as much as they would at target or Vons.
You're better off getting drinks somewhere else.<//review>

Update 10-11-19: I hired a disabled veteran to do repairs around my house. He was parked on the street in front of my place while I was at work. I got a call from management demanding to know why there was a car parked outside my house. I told them about the repairs and was immediately informed that he cannot park there. I explained that he was working on the driveway and wasn't able to park there and I told her he was disabled and wouldn't be able to walk from the clubhouse to my space. She threatened to have him towed. I called him and let him know the situation. Later, I got another call from management. They were concerned I was painting using an unapproved color scheme. I reminded them that this was the one approved about a year and a half ago and informed them I was just touching up in some spots. The call escalated rapidly and I was so frustrated that, yes, I did use a couple of F bombs to describe how ridiculous this was. I was told that my house was the worst on the block and I asked how I could possibly be worse than the home two spaces down that had blue tarps held down by bricks on their roof. She then told me it was none of my business and threatened to have me evicted because I cursed at her. Mind you, I did say that this is f-ing b.s. BUT I never called her names or threatened her at all. In the end, she made us repaint the entire house in a new color, costing hundreds more in labor and supplies. The house down the street still has blue tarps almost a year later. There is definitely favoritism going on. I've lived here 30 years and have had to deal with this kind of nepotism year after year.

As for safety, our new neighbors seem to bring a few meth addicts around at night, our stuff has been stolen from the driveway (again) and someone attempted to break in through my back door, breaking the door in the process.

Oh! And one of those guys from next door stopped us one afternoon to ask if he could come in to charge his phone. He said he couldn't go home to do it since he's been on the run for a few days and admitted to using a little meth to keep his head right. I don't know if it is the same person who tried going into my driveway at night last week. I startled him as much as he did me since I was in my parked car on the phone at the time.

Although located midst of predominantly Spanish speaking population, this ‚Äúfast-food‚Äù joint produces yum-yum Thai cuisine. The food was flavorful that included the spiciness, tanginess, saltiness, bitterness, and sweetness.

< Review>
Hands down my favorite Thai restaurant in SA!! Love this place, make sure you get a reservation in advance because even if you do, there will be a small wait still! Parking is quite easy, plenty outside. Service is good, most of the servers are Thai and they do this birthday singing if it's your bday! I have tried a lot of things from their menu: wings, sausage, papaya salad (pretty spicy), pad thai, hat Yai fried chicken (which I thought its good but not that special, red curry, red curry, fried fish, their special beef noodle soup and their shaved ice dessert which is bomb!!<//Review>
